<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Programmatic scrolling to edges or coordinates</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Scroll position and overflow state helpers</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Scrollbar state for styling (<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hovering</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrolling</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hidden</code>)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Horizontal and vertical scrollbar support</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>To set up the scroll area correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and
how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<p>It&#x27;s important to note that the scroll area requires the following styles to be
applied to the viewport element to hide the scrollbar:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scope</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scroll-area&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;viewport&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* hide scrollbar */</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">scrollbar-width</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> none<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token selector">&amp;<span class="token pseudo-element">::-webkit-scrollbar</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token property">display</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> none<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the scroll area package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> scrollArea</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/scroll-area&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The scroll area package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<div data-scope="tabs" data-part="root" id="tabs:scroll-area/usage.mdx" data-orientation="horizontal" dir="ltr" class="w_full max-w_768px bd-w_1px my_8 bg_bg.code.block bdr_6px"><div data-scope="tabs" <h3 id="programmatic-scrolling-to-edges" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic scrolling to edges<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-scrolling-to-edges"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>You can programmatically scroll to any edge of the scroll area using the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToEdge</code> method:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scroll to bottom</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">scrollToEdge</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">edge</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;bottom&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scroll to top with custom easing</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">scrollToEdge</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">edge</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;top&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">duration</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">500</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function-variable function">easing</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">t</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> t <span class="token operator">*</span> t<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-scrolling-to-coordinates" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic scrolling to coordinates<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-scrolling-to-coordinates"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollTo</code> method to scroll to specific coordinates:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scroll to specific position</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">scrollTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">top</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">100</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">left</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">50</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Scroll with smooth behavior</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">scrollTo</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">top</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">behavior</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;smooth&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">duration</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">300</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="reading-scroll-position-and-overflow" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Reading scroll position and overflow<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#reading-scroll-position-and-overflow"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The API provides several properties to check the current scroll state:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Check if at edges</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">isAtTop</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">isAtBottom</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">isAtLeft</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">isAtRight</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Check for overflow</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">hasOverflowX</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">hasOverflowY</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// boolean</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Get scroll progress (0-1)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> progress <span class="token operator">=</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getScrollProgress</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// { x: number, y: number }</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="rendering-scrollbars-only-when-needed" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Rendering scrollbars only when needed<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rendering-scrollbars-only-when-needed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Only render scrollbars when there&#x27;s overflow content:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">hasOverflowY</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getScrollbarProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getThumbProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">hasOverflowX</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getScrollbarProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">      </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getThumbProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>div</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="scrollbar-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Scrollbar state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#scrollbar-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Get the current state of a scrollbar for styling purposes:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> verticalState <span class="token operator">=</span> api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getScrollbarState</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">// Returns: { hovering: boolean, scrolling: boolean, hidden: boolean }</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="scrolling-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Scrolling state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#scrolling-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the user is actively scrolling, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-scrolling</code> attribute is set on the
scrollbar elements:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scrollbar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scrolling</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles when actively scrolling */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;thumb&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-scrolling</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for thumb when scrolling */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="hover-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Hover state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#hover-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When hovering over the scroll area or scrollbar, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-hover</code> attribute is
applied:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-hover</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles when hovering over scroll area */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scrollbar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-hover</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles when hovering over scrollbar */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="hidden-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Hidden state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#hidden-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Scrollbars can be automatically hidden when not needed:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scrollbar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-hidden</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for hidden scrollbar */</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">opacity</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token property">pointer-events</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> none<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Different styles can be applied based on scrollbar orientation:</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scrollbar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* vertical scrollbar styles */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;scrollbar&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;horizontal&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* horizontal scrollbar styles */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>The scroll area&#x27;s <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods and properties:</p>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The scroll area machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; viewport: string; content: string; scrollbar: string; thumb: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the scroll area elements</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The scroll area <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isAtTop</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area is at the top</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isAtBottom</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area is at the bottom</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isAtLeft</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area is at the left</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">isAtRight</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area is at the right</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hasOverflowX</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area has horizontal overflow</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">hasOverflowY</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the scroll area has vertical overflow</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getScrollProgress</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; Point</code><span class="d_block">Get the scroll progress as values between 0 and 1</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollToEdge</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ScrollToEdgeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Scroll to the edge of the scroll area</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">scrollTo</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ScrollToDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Scroll to specific scrollbar</span></li></ul>

likely forgot to import, pass, or provide it.\")}"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"12:T1292,"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"A scroll area provides a custom-scrollbar viewport for overflow content.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"ScrollArea\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Programmatic scrolling to edges or coordinates\n- Scroll position and overflow state helpers\n- Scrollbar state for styling (`hovering`, `scrolling`, `hidden`)\n- Horizontal and vertical scrollbar support\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the scroll area package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"scroll-area/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the scroll area correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and\nhow we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n## Required style\n\nIt's important to note that the scroll area requires the following styles to be\napplied to the viewport element to hide the scrollbar:\n\n```css\n[data-scope=\"scroll-area\"][data-part=\"viewport\"] {\n  /* hide scrollbar */\n  scrollbar-width: none;\n  \u0026::-webkit-scrollbar {\n    display: none;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the scroll area package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as scrollArea from \"@zag-js/scroll-area\"\n```\n\nThe scroll area package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"scroll-area/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Programmatic scrolling to edges\n\nYou can programmatically scroll to any edge of the scroll area using the\n`scrollToEdge` method:\n\n```jsx\n// Scroll to bottom\napi.scrollToEdge({ edge: \"bottom\" })\n\n// Scroll to top with custom easing\napi.scrollToEdge({\n  edge: \"top\",\n  duration: 500,\n  easing: (t) =\u003e t * t,\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic scrolling to coordinates\n\nUse the `scrollTo` method to scroll to specific coordinates:\n\n```jsx\n// Scroll to specific position\napi.scrollTo({\n  top: 100,\n  left: 50,\n})\n\n// Scroll with smooth behavior\napi.scrollTo({\n  top: 200,\n  behavior: \"smooth\",\n  duration: 300,\n})\n```\n\n### Reading scroll position and overflow\n\nThe API provides several properties to check the current scroll state:\n\n```jsx\n// Check if at edges\nconsole.log(api.isAtTop) // boolean\nconsole.log(api.isAtBottom) // boolean\nconsole.log(api.isAtLeft) // boolean\nconsole.log(api.isAtRight) // boolean\n\n// Check for overflow\nconsole.log(api.hasOverflowX) // boolean\nconsole.log(api.hasOverflowY) // boolean\n\n// Get scroll progress (0-1)\nconst progress = api.getScrollProgress() // { x: number, y: number }\n```\n\n### Rendering scrollbars only when needed\n\nOnly render scrollbars when there's overflow content:\n\n```jsx\n{\n  api.hasOverflowY \u0026\u0026 (\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getScrollbarProps({ orientation: \"vertical\" })}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv {...api.getThumbProps({ orientation: \"vertical\" })} /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n{\n  api.hasOverflowX \u0026\u0026 (\n    \u003cdiv {...api.getScrollbarProps({ orientation: \"horizontal\" })}\u003e\n      \u003cdiv {...api.getThumbProps({ orientation: \"horizontal\" })} /\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n```\n\n### Scrollbar state\n\nGet the current state of a scrollbar for styling purposes:\n\n```jsx\nconst verticalState = api.getScrollbarState({ orientation: \"vertical\" })\n// Returns: { hovering: boolean, scrolling: boolean, hidden: boolean }\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Scrolling state\n\nWhen the user is actively scrolling, a `data-scrolling` attribute is set on the\nscrollbar elements:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"scrollbar\"][data-scrolling] {\n  /* styles when actively scrolling */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"thumb\"][data-scrolling] {\n  /* styles for thumb when scrolling */\n}\n```\n\n### Hover state\n\nWhen hovering over the scroll area or scrollbar, a `data-hover` attribute is\napplied:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-hover] {\n  /* styles when hovering over scroll area */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"scrollbar\"][data-hover] {\n  /* styles when hovering over scrollbar */\n}\n```\n\n### Hidden state\n\nScrollbars can be automatically hidden when not needed:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"scrollbar\"][data-hidden] {\n  /* styles for hidden scrollbar */\n  opacity: 0;\n  pointer-events: none;\n}\n```\n\n### Orientation\n\nDifferent styles can be applied based on scrollbar orientation:\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"scrollbar\"][data-orientation=\"vertical\"] {\n  /* vertical scrollbar styles */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"scrollbar\"][data-orientation=\"horizontal\"] {\n  /* horizontal scrollbar styles */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\nThe scroll area's `api` exposes the following methods and properties:\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe scroll area machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe scroll area `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"scroll-area\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Scroll Area\",\"description\":\"Using the scroll area machine in your
